{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_10","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nbase=Path('/app')\n# parse maintenance reports\nrecords=[]\nfor path in sorted((base/'raw_service_reports').rglob('*_service.txt')):\n    txt=path.read_text().strip().splitlines()\n    data={}\n    for line in txt:\n        if ':' in line:\n            k,v=line.split(':',1)\n            data[k.strip()] = v.strip()\n    records.append({\n        'work_order_id': data['WORK ORDER'],\n        'machine_id': data['MACHINE'],\n        'technician_id': data['TECHNICIAN'],\n        'work_type': data['WORK TYPE'],\n        'reported_reason': data['REPORTED REASON'],\n        'day': int(data['DAY']),\n        'started': data['STARTED'],\n        'completed': data['COMPLETED'],\n        'report_path': str(path.relative_to(base)),\n    })\nmaint=pd.DataFrame(records)\n# create timestamps in minutes from day 0\nfor col in ['started','completed']:\n    hhmm=maint[col].str.split(':', expand=True).astype(int)\n    maint[col+'_min']=maint['day']*24*60 + hhmm[0]*60 + hhmm[1]\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min','work_order_id']).reset_index(drop=True)\nmaint['next_completed_min']=maint.groupby('machine_id')['completed_min'].shift(-1)\nmaint['next_work_order_id']=maint.groupby('machine_id')['work_order_id'].shift(-1)\n\npb=pd.read_csv(base/'production_batches.csv')\nmal=pd.read_csv(base/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nqi=pd.read_csv(base/'quality_inspections.csv')\nproducts=pd.read_csv(base/'products.csv')\n\n# production start timestamps\nhhmm=mal['start_time'].str.split(':', expand=True).astype(int)\nmal['start_min']=mal['day']*24*60 + hhmm[0]*60 + hhmm[1]\nhhmm2=mal['end_time'].str.split(':', expand=True).astype(int)\nmal['end_min']=mal['day']*24*60 + hhmm2[0]*60 + hhmm2[1]\n\nbatches=pb.merge(mal[['job_id','day','machine_id','start_min','end_min','sequence_on_machine']], left_on=['job_id','production_day','machine_id'], right_on=['job_id','day','machine_id'], how='left')\nassert batches['start_min'].notna().all()\n\n# link each batch to most recent maintenance on same machine completed before start\nlinked=[]\nfor machine_id, g in batches.sort_values(['machine_id','start_min']).groupby('machine_id', sort=False):\n    mg=maint[maint.machine_id==machine_id][['work_order_id','technician_id','work_type','reported_reason','completed_min','next_completed_min']].sort_values('completed_min')\n    if mg.empty:\n        tmp=g.copy()\n        tmp['work_order_id']=pd.NA\n        tmp['technician_id']=pd.NA\n        tmp['work_type']=pd.NA\n        tmp['reported_reason']=pd.NA\n        tmp['maintenance_completed_min']=pd.NA\n        tmp['next_completed_min']=pd.NA\n        linked.append(tmp)\n        continue\n    # merge_asof\n    tmp=pd.merge_asof(g.sort_values('start_min'), mg, left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward')\n    linked.append(tmp)\nlinked=pd.concat(linked, ignore_index=True)\nlinked=linked.merge(qi[['batch_id','inspection_day','rejected_quantity','rejected_pct','defect_code','inspection_result']], on='batch_id', how='left')\nlinked=linked.merge(products[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id', how='left')\n\nprint('batches without prior maintenance', linked['work_order_id'].isna().sum())\nrej=linked[linked.inspection_result=='REJECTED'].copy()\nprint('rejected linked to work orders', rej['work_order_id'].notna().sum(), 'of', len(rej))\n\n# counts by linked work order\nwo_stats=linked.groupby(['work_order_id','technician_id','machine_id']).agg(\n    total_batches=('batch_id','size'),\n    rejected_batches=('inspection_result', lambda s: (s=='REJECTED').sum()),\n    products=('product_id','nunique'),\n    rejected_products=('product_id', lambda s: s[linked.loc[s.index,'inspection_result']=='REJECTED'].nunique()),\n).reset_index()\nwo_stats=wo_stats.sort_values(['rejected_batches','total_batches'], ascending=[False,False])\nprint('\\\\nTop work orders by rejected batches:')\nprint(wo_stats.head(40).to_string(index=False))\n\ntech_stats=rej.groupby('technician_id').agg(rejected_batches=('batch_id','nunique'), work_orders=('work_order_id','nunique'), products=('product_id','nunique'), machines=('machine_id','nunique')).sort_values('rejected_batches', ascending=False)\nprint('\\\\nTop technicians by linked rejected batches:')\nprint(tech_stats.head(20).to_string())\n\nprint('\\\\nRejected defect counts by work order top 20:')\nfor wo in wo_stats.head(20)['work_order_id']:\n    sub=rej[rej.work_order_id==wo]\n    if sub.empty: continue\n    print(wo, 'tech', sub['technician_id'].iloc[0], 'machine', sub['machine_id'].iloc[0], 'rejected', len(sub), 'products', sorted(sub['product_id'].unique()), 'defects', sub['defect_code'].value_counts().to_dict())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

tech_to_products={t:sorted(det[det['technician_id']==t]['product_id'].unique()) for t in confirmed}\n    print('\\\\nMODE', mode)\n    for t,p in tech_to_products.items():\n
